  490. Well made, excellent price, fast delivery. I use these for travel as they are low cost and I don't have to worry about losing them. Sold as more or less disposable, they are reusable. The Plackers are small, and low profile, but being small do sometimes fall out of place during sleep, usually just on one side or the other. I use the guard to combat the effects of night clenching, which includes broken teeth and headaches in the morning. These do help. For day to day I use the Sleep Right Dental Guard, which is larger, and the bite wings pivot, so it is actually a three-part guard. I don't generally have a problem with the Sleep Right falling out, but the Sleep Right is extremely expensive and it is hard to understand why it costs so much. Either is much better than the very expensive custom bite guard from the dentist, which I am convince led to another broken tooth. Plackers work by putting a bit wing between the molars, which prevents excessive pressure. My dentist explained that the bit wing should not have excessive squishyness, as that trains the sleeper to repetitively bite down; rather the proper bite wing should be soft enough to not damage teeth but hard enough to train the sleeping brain to not bite. The bit wings on the Plackers are thin silicone, which seems to fit the bill. If you wonder whether a bite guard will help you, this is a very reasonable priced item and makes either a low-cost experiment or for permanent use. BTW, I did not know for years that I was biting at night, I don't grind, just clench, so my wife never knew. What finally clued my dentist in was receding gums, which he said was due to clenching, and finally breaking some teeth. Literally cracking them to pieces due to the repetitive and extreme pressure. Talk to your dentist if you are waking up with headaches around the back of your head and sore jaw, teeth or gums. This turns out to be a serious and expensive dental issue if you don't take preventive measures.
